import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys

def main():
    if len(sys.argv) != 2:
        print("Must be open with a filename")
        exit()
    filename = sys.argv[1].encode('ascii')
    context = zmq.Context()
    socket = context.socker(zmq.REQ)
    socket.connect("tcp://localhost:5555")
    response = socket.send(filename)
    print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))
    with open(filename, "rb") as file:
        data = file.read()
        socket.send(data)
        response = socket.recv()
        print("Reply [%s ]" %(response))

if __name__=='__main__':
    main()
    import zmq, sys
